● Update(flora_translate/chemistry_agent.py)
  ⎿  Added 48 lines
      138  """
      139  
      140  
      141 +def _normalize_plan_data(data: dict) -> dict:                 
      142 +    """Fix common LLM output deviations before Pydantic valida
          +tion.                                                         
      143 +                                                              
      144 +    The LLM sometimes returns fields in slightly different sha
          +pes                                                           
      145 +    than the schema expects. This normalizes them.            
      146 +    """                                                       
      147 +    # incompatible_pairs: expected [[A, B], ...] but LLM may r
          +eturn                                                         
      148 +    # [{"species_1": A, "species_2": B, ...}, ...]            
      149 +    pairs = data.get("incompatible_pairs", [])                
      150 +    if pairs and isinstance(pairs[0], dict):                  
      151 +        normalized = []                                       
      152 +        for p in pairs:                                       
      153 +            if isinstance(p, dict):                           
      154 +                # Extract the two species from whatever keys t
          +he LLM used                                                   
      155 +                vals = [v for k, v in p.items() if isinstance(
          +v, str) and k != "reason" and k != "reasoning"]               
      156 +                if len(vals) >= 2:                            
      157 +                    normalized.append(vals[:2])               
      158 +                elif vals:                                    
      159 +                    normalized.append(vals)                   
      160 +            else:                                             
      161 +                normalized.append(p)                          
      162 +        data["incompatible_pairs"] = normalized               
      163 +                                                              
      164 +    # stream_logic: expected list of dicts with stream_label/r
          +eagents/reasoning                                             
      165 +    # but LLM may nest differently                            
      166 +    streams = data.get("stream_logic", [])                    
      167 +    if streams and isinstance(streams[0], dict):              
      168 +        for s in streams:                                     
      169 +            # reagents should be a list of strings            
      170 +            r = s.get("reagents", [])                         
      171 +            if r and isinstance(r[0], dict):                  
      172 +                s["reagents"] = [                             
      173 +                    item.get("name", str(item)) for item in r 
      174 +                ]                                             
      175 +                                                              
      176 +    # mechanism_steps: species_involved should be list[str]   
      177 +    steps = data.get("mechanism_steps", [])                   
      178 +    for step in steps:                                        
      179 +        if isinstance(step, dict):                            
      180 +            sp = step.get("species_involved", [])             
      181 +            if sp and isinstance(sp[0], dict):                
      182 +                step["species_involved"] = [                  
      183 +                    item.get("name", str(item)) for item in sp
      184 +                ]                                             
      185 +                                                              
      186 +    return data                                               
      187 +                                                              
      188 +                                                              
      189  class ChemistryReasoningAgent:
      190      """Layer 1: Pure chemistry analysis before any hardware de
           cisions."""

  But the schema expects [["Base", "substrate"]]. The normalizer now converts

● Here's a good test case — a well-known photochemistry reaction with clear
  batch conditions:

  Test Input (paste this into FLORA-Translate)

  Photoredox-catalyzed decarboxylative radical addition of α-amino acids to
  Michael acceptors. Batch conditions: fac-Ir(ppy)3 (1 mol%) as photocatalyst,
  N-Boc-proline (1.0 equiv) as radical precursor, methyl vinyl ketone (2.0
  equiv)
  as Michael acceptor, K2HPO4 (1.5 equiv) as base, DMF as solvent, 0.1 M
  concentration, room temperature (25°C), 450 nm blue LED irradiation,
  N2 atmosphere (degassed by freeze-pump-thaw), 24 hours reaction time,
  72% isolated yield, 0.5 mmol scale.

  Why this is a good test case

  1. Well-studied reaction — lots of literature on photoredox decarboxylation in
   flow
  2. Clear mechanism — Ir(III) oxidative quenching cycle, CO2 extrusion, radical
   addition. The Chemistry Agent should identify all of this
  3. Multiple species — photocatalyst, radical precursor, Michael acceptor,
  base, solvent — the agent must assign each to a stream
  4. Clear stream separation logic — the proline + Ir(ppy)3 should be in one
  stream (SET requires proximity), the Michael acceptor can be separate
  5. O2-sensitive — the agent should flag deoxygenation
  6. 24h → flow should be ~5-15 min — you can check if the intensification
  factor makes sense
  7. Known flow translations exist — MacMillan, Noël, and others have published
  flow versions of this exact reaction class

  What to check in the output

  ┌──────────────────┬─────────────────────────────┬────────────────────────┐
  │      Check       │      What to look for       │        Red flag        │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Chemistry Plan — │ All 5 species named         │ Missing proline or     │
  │  species         │ correctly with roles        │ calling it "reagent 1" │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Chemistry Plan — │ Oxidative quenching,        │ Wrong cycle (reductive │
  │  mechanism       │ decarboxylation step,       │  quenching) or missing │
  │                  │ radical addition            │  CO2 loss              │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Chemistry Plan — │ Proline + Ir(ppy)3          │ Everything in one      │
  │  streams         │ together, MVK separate      │ stream, or catalyst    │
  │                  │                             │ with MVK               │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Chemistry Plan — │ Flags oxygen-sensitive =    │ Misses it              │
  │  O2              │ true                        │                        │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Wavelength       │ 450 nm (matches Ir(ppy)3    │ 530 nm or mismatched   │
  │                  │ absorption)                 │                        │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │                  │                             │ >60 min (too           │
  │ Residence time   │ 5-20 min range              │ conservative) or <1    │
  │                  │                             │ min (unrealistic)      │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Deoxygenation    │ Present (N2 sparging or     │ Missing entirely       │
  │                  │ degassing)                  │                        │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ BPR              │ ~5 bar (DMF bp is 153°C, RT │ 50 bar (overkill)      │
  │                  │  reaction, so low BPR ok)   │                        │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Tubing           │ FEP or PFA, 1.0 mm ID       │ SS (opaque — bad for   │
  │                  │                             │ photochem)             │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Post-reactor     │ No quench needed (no excess │ Unnecessary quench     │
  │                  │  oxidant)                   │ step                   │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Council          │ ChemistryValidator passes,  │ REJECT on wavelength   │
  │                  │ no REJECT                   │ or missing degas       │
  └──────────────────┴─────────────────────────────┴────────────────────────┘

  If you want a harder test after this one, try something more obscure where
  your corpus probably has no close match — like a photochemical Paternò-Büchi
  oxetane formation or a visible-light mediated C-H fluorination. That will test
   how the agent behaves at LOW confidence.

❯ ok for this translate module. we need to add another feature. this feature is 
 process suggestion. refer to below and add it to the flora agent overal        
layout. this module. ========================================================== 
======================                                                          
                                                                                
FLORA-DESIGN MODULE — Complete Implementation Guideline                         
                                                                                
For Claude Code Agent — chemistry context + full technical specification        
                                                                                
Module name: flora_design                                                       
                                                                                
Version: 1.0 | March 2026                                                       
=============================================================================== 
=                                                                               
                                                                                
SECTION 0 — WHAT THIS MODULE DOES                                               
FLORA-Design takes a free-text chemistry goal from the user (e.g., "Help me     
                                                                                
design the flow synthesis of a Ru-photocatalyzed radical addition") and         
returns:                                                                        
1.    A complete, physically validated flow process design                      
                                                                                
(unit operations, conditions, reactor configuration)                            
2.    A static process flow diagram (SVG/PNG, manuscript quality)               
3.    An interactive visual in the Streamlit dashboard                          
4.    A human-readable explanation grounded in your literature corpus           
It combines two strategies:                                                     
·    Strategy 2: Feature-driven unit operation selection (rule-based + LLM)     
·    Strategy 3: RAG-based topology generation and parameter assignment         
This module is DIFFERENT from FLORA-Translate:                                  
·    FLORA-Translate: "I have a batch protocol → convert it to flow"            
·    FLORA-Design:    "I have a chemistry goal → design me a flow process"      
The same ChromaDB corpus (140 photochemistry JSONs) powers both modules.        
                                                                                
The same ENGINE council validates both outputs.                                 
=============================================================================== 
=                                                                               
                                                                                
SECTION 1 — FILE STRUCTURE                                                      
The module lives alongside flora_translate/ in the same project.                
flora_design/                                                                   
                                                                                
├── main.py                        # entry point: design(goal_text) ->          
DesignResult                                                                    
                                                                                
├── chemistry_classifier.py        # ChemistryClassifier: free text →           
ChemFeatures                                                                    
                                                                                
├── unit_op_selector.py            # UnitOpSelector: ChemFeatures → UnitOpList  
                                                                                
├── topology_agent.py              # TopologyAgent: RAG → ProcessTopology       
                                                                                
├── parameter_agent.py             # ParameterAgent: RAG → filled parameters    
                                                                                
├── visualizer/                                                                 
                                                                                
│   ├── init.py                                                                 
                                                                                
│   ├── flowsheet_builder.py       # builds pyflowsheet diagram → SVG/PNG       
                                                                                
│   ├── symbols.py                 # custom flow chemistry unit operation       
symbols                                                                         
                                                                                
│   ├── streamlit_diagram.py       # Streamlit-compatible interactive diagram   
                                                                                
│   └── plot_builder.py            # ΔP vs flow rate, yield vs residence time   
plots                                                                           
                                                                                
├── prompts/                                                                    
                                                                                
│   ├── classify_system.txt

ilding, verify these test cases manually:                                       
Test 1 — Chemistry classifier:                                                  
                                                                                
Input: "Design me a flow process for Ir(ppy)3-catalyzed [2+2] cycloaddition"    
                                                                                
Expected: reaction_class="photocycloaddition", photocatalyst="Ir(ppy)3",        
                                                                                
wavelength_nm=450, O2_sensitive=True                                            
Test 2 — Unit op selector:                                                      
                                                                                
Input: ChemFeatures with O2_sensitive=True, generates_gas=False, T=25°C,        
                                                                                
solvent="MeCN" (bp=82°C)                                                        
                                                                                
Expected: pump_a, pump_b, mixer, deoxygenation, coil_reactor, led_module,       
                                                                                
collector. NO BPR (T < bp - 20 = 62°C).                                         
Test 3 — Consistency check:                                                     
                                                                                
Input: residence_time_min=10, flow_rate=0.5 mL/min                              
                                                                                
Expected: reactor_volume = 5.0 mL, tubing_length ≈ 6.4 m (for 1.0mm ID)         
Test 4 — Fluidics Agent:                                                        
                                                                                
Input: flow_rate=1.0 mL/min, ID=1.0mm, length=6.4m, viscosity=0.37cP (MeCN)

Test 5 — Full pipeline:

in 1–2 rounds, confidence=HIGH or MEDIUM                                        
Test 6 — Streamlit:                                                             
                                                                                
Run: streamlit run app.py                                                       
                                                                                
Verify: both FLORA-Design and FLORA-Translate tabs load without error,          
                                                                                
form submission triggers spinner, results display in 4 tabs,                    
                                                                                
PNG download button works.                                                      
=============================================================================== 
=                                                                               
                                                                                
SECTION 13 — KNOWN LIMITATIONS TO DOCUMENT IN MANUSCRIPT                        
1.    The rule-based UnitOpSelector covers only photochemistry-specific unit    
ops.                                                                            
                                                                                
Extension to other chemistries (Grignard, nitration) requires adding new        
                                                                                
rules to UNIT_OP_RULES — this is by design, not a bug.                          
2.    pyflowsheet auto-layout can produce overlapping nodes for >8 unit ops.    
                                                                                
For complex multi-step processes, manual position overrides may be needed.      
                                                                                
A React Flow frontend (v2) will solve this with drag-and-drop layout.           
3.    The alternative topology generation depends on the LLM finding a          
                                                                                
meaningfully different option. For very constrained chemistries, the            
                                                                                
alternative may be similar to the primary. Flag this in the output.             
4.    Solvent viscosity affects ΔP calculation significantly. Unknown solvents  
                                                                                
default to η=1.0 cP with a WARNING flag — chemist must verify.                  
5.    Yield vs. residence time plot is populated only if retrieved records      
report                                                                          
                                                                                
both fields. For many papers, yield is reported but residence time is not,      
                                                                                
leaving the plot sparse. This is a corpus quality issue, not a code issue.      
=============================================================================== 
=                                                                               
                                                                                
END OF GUIDELINE

● Everything is built. Here's the summary:

  FLORA-Design — ~2,000 lines across 19 files

  Pipeline:
  "Design a Ru-catalyzed radical addition flow process"
          │
          ▼
  [1] ChemistryClassifier (LLM + rule-based post-processing)
          → ChemFeatures: reaction_class, catalyst, wavelength, sensitivities
          │
          ▼
  [2] UnitOpSelector (pure rules, no LLM)
          → pump_a, pump_b, mixer, deoxygenation, coil_reactor, LED, collector
          │
          ▼
  [3] TopologyAgent (RAG + LLM)
          → Retrieves 5 similar papers from ChromaDB
          → Generates primary + alternative topology with stream connections
          │
          ▼
  [4] ParameterAgent
          → Fills residence_time, flow_rate, reactor_volume, tubing dimensions
          → Consistency check: τ × Q = V
          │
          ▼
  [5] ENGINE council (shared with FLORA-Translate)
          → Kinetics, Fluidics, Safety, Chemistry validation
          │
          ▼
  [6] FlowsheetBuilder
          → SVG process flow diagram (pure SVG, no external dependencies)
          → PNG if cairosvg installed
          │
          ▼
  [7] DesignResult with explanation, alternatives, warnings

  Key design decisions:
  - Shares schemas.py, config.py, engine/, ChromaDB, and lab_inventory with
  FLORA-Translate (no code duplication)
  - UnitOpSelector is rule-based — deterministic, no LLM, fast
  - SVG generator is custom — no pyflowsheet dependency; produces clean diagrams
   directly
  - BPR logic is correct: only added when T > solvent_bp - 20°C or gas generated
   (verified: MeCN at 25°C = no BPR needed)

  Streamlit app now has 4 modules in the sidebar:
  - FLORA-Design (new)
  - FLORA-Translate
  - FLORA-Extract
  - Knowledge Base

  To run:
  # CLI
  python -m flora_design.main "Ru(bpy)3 photoredox radical addition in MeCN at 
  RT"

  # GUI
  streamlit run app.py

  Optional: pip install cairosvg plotly for PNG export and interactive plots in
  the dashboard.

● Fixed. The problem was cairosvg crashing on SVG <marker> elements (a known
  cairosvg bug). Changes:

  1. Removed the <defs><marker> element that caused the crash
  2. Replaced marker-end="url(#arrowhead)" with inline triangle polygons
  3. Added a catch-all except Exception so PNG failures never block the pipeline

  Try running it again — the SVG will render in the Streamlit app directly, and
  PNG will work too now.

       65      return "\n\n".join(blocks)

       67  
       68 +def _normalize_topology_data(data: dict) -> dict:             
       69 +    """Fix common LLM output shape deviations before Pydantic 
          +validation."""                                                
       70 +    # literature_support: expected list[str] but LLM may retur
          +n list[dict]                                                  
       71 +    support = data.get("literature_support", [])              
       72 +    if support and isinstance(support[0], dict):              
       73 +        normalized = []                                       
       74 +        for item in support:                                  
       75 +            if isinstance(item, dict):                        
       76 +                # Extract DOI or any string value from the dic
          +t                                                             
       77 +                doi = item.get("doi") or item.get("DOI") or it
          +em.get("record")                                              
       78 +                if doi:                                       
       79 +                    normalized.append(str(doi))               
       80 +                else:                                         
       81 +                    # Fall back to first string value found   
       82 +                    for v in item.values():                   
       83 +                        if isinstance(v, str):                
       84 +                            normalized.append(v)              
       85 +                            break                             
       86 +            else:                                             
       87 +                normalized.append(str(item))                  
       88 +        data["literature_support"] = normalized               
       89 +                                                              
       90 +    # streams: StreamConnection fields may come with wrong key
          + names                                                        
       91 +    streams = data.get("streams", [])                         
       92 +    for s in streams:                                         
       93 +        if isinstance(s, dict):                               
       94 +            # LLM sometimes uses "source"/"target" instead of 
          +"from_op"/"to_op"                                             
       95 +            if "source" in s and "from_op" not in s:          
       96 +                s["from_op"] = s.pop("source")                
       97 +            if "target" in s and "to_op" not in s:            
       98 +                s["to_op"] = s.pop("target")                  
       99 +            if "from" in s and "from_op" not in s:            
      100 +                s["from_op"] = s.pop("from")                  
      101 +            if "to" in s and "to_op" not in s:                
      102 +                s["to_op"] = s.pop("to")                      
      103 +                                                              
      104 +    return data                                               
      105 +                                                              
      106 +                                                              
      107  class TopologyAgent:
      108      """Use RAG to refine unit operations and generate process 
           topology."""

       45 +# ------------------------------------------------------------

       46 +# Chemistry-aware topology builder                            
       47 +# ------------------------------------------------------------
          +---------------                                               
       48 +                                                              
       49 +def _build_translate_topology(                                
       50 +    proposal: FlowProposal,                                   
       51 +    chemistry_plan: ChemistryPlan | None,                     
       52 +    batch_record: BatchRecord,                                
       53 +) -> ProcessTopology:                                         
       54 +    """Convert a validated FlowProposal + ChemistryPlan into a
          + ProcessTopology.                                             
       55 +                                                              
       56 +    All pump nodes carry the actual chemical names and concent
          +rations from the                                              
       57 +    proposal's stream assignments. Every node has chemistry-ri
          +ch parameters so                                              
       58 +    the flowsheet diagram shows real chemistry, not generic la
          +bels.                                                         
       59 +    """                                                       
       60 +    ops: list[UnitOperation] = []                             
       61 +    streams: list[StreamConnection] = []                      
       62 +    stream_counter = [0]                                      
       63 +                                                              
       64 +    def next_stream(from_op, to_op, label=""):                
       65 +        stream_counter[0] += 1                                
       66 +        sid = f"s{stream_counter[0]}"                         
       67 +        streams.append(StreamConnection(                      
       68 +            stream_id=sid, from_op=from_op,                   
       69 +            to_op=to_op, stream_type="liquid", label=label    
       70 +        ))                                                    
       71 +        return sid                                            
       72 +                                                              
       73 +    # ── Pumps from stream assignments ───────────────────────
          +──────────────────                                            
       74 +    pump_ids = []                                             
       75 +    if proposal.streams:                                      
       76 +        for s in proposal.streams:                            
       77 +            op_id = f"pump_{s.stream_label.lower()}"          
       78 +            ops.append(UnitOperation(                         
       79 +                op_id=op_id,                                  
       80 +                op_type="pump",                               
       81 +                label=f"Pump {s.stream_label} — {s.pump_role}"
          +,                                                             
       82 +                parameters={                                  
       83 +                    "stream": s.stream_label,                 
       84 +                    "contents": s.contents,                   
       85 +                    "solvent": s.solvent,                     
       86 +                    "concentration_M": s.concentration_M,     
       87 +                    "flow_rate_mL_min": s.flow_rate_mL_min,   
       88 +                },                                            
       89 +                required=True,                                
       90 +                rationale=s.reasoning or f"Stream {s.stream_la
          +bel}",                                                        
       91 +            ))                                                
       92 +            pump_ids.append(op_id)                            
       93 +    else:                                                     
       94 +        # Fallback: generic pumps                             
       95 +        for label in ("A", "B"):                              
       96 +            op_id = f"pump_{label.lower()}"                   
       97 +            ops.append(UnitOperation(                         
       98 +                op_id=op_id, op_type="pump",                  
       99 +                label=f"Pump {label}",                        
      100 +                parameters={"stream": f"reagent_{label}"},    
      101 +                required=True, rationale="Reagent delivery",  
      102 +            ))                                                
      103 +            pump_ids.append(op_id)                            
      104 +                                                              
      105 +    # ── Mixer ───────────────────────────────────────────────
          +──────────────────                                            
      106 +    ops.append(UnitOperation(                                 
      107 +        op_id="mixer_1", op_type="mixer",                     
      108 +        label=proposal.mixer_type or "T-Mixer",               
      109 +        parameters={                                          
      110 +            "type": proposal.mixer_type or "T-mixer",         
      111 +            "material": "PEEK",                               
      112 +        },                                                    
      113 +        required=True,                                        
      114 +        rationale=proposal.mixing_order_reasoning or "Combine 
          +streams",                                                     
      115 +    ))                                                        
      116 +    for pid in pump_ids:                                      
      117 +        next_stream(pid, "mixer_1")                           
      118 +                                                              
      119 +    prev_op = "mixer_1"                                       
      120 +                                                              
      121 +    # ── Pre-reactor steps (deoxygenation etc.) ──────────────
          +───────────────────                                           
      122 +    deoxy_method = proposal.deoxygenation_method              
      123 +    if not deoxy_method and chemistry_plan and chemistry_plan.
          +deoxygenation_required:                                       
      124 +        deoxy_method = "N2 sparging"                          
      125 +                                                              
      126 +    pre_steps = proposal.pre_reactor_steps or []              
      127 +    degas_in_pre = any(                                       
      128 +        "degas" in s.lower() or "deoxy" in s.lower() or "sparg
          +" in s.lower()                                                
      129 +        for s in pre_steps                                    
      130 +    )                                                         
      131 +                                                              
      132 +    if deoxy_method or degas_in_pre:                          
      133 +        method_label = deoxy_method or "N2 sparging"          
      134 +        # Find fuller description from pre_reactor_steps if av
          +ailable                                                       
      135 +        for step in pre_steps:                                
      136 +            if "degas" in step.lower() or "sparg" in step.lowe
          +r():                                                          
      137 +                method_label = step                           
      138 +                break                                         
      139 +        ops.append(UnitOperation(                             
      140 +            op_id="deoxy_1", op_type="deoxygenation_unit",    
      141 +            label="Inline Deoxygenation",                     
      142 +            parameters={"method": method_label},              
      143 +            required=True,                                    
      144 +            rationale=(chemistry_plan.deoxygenation_reasoning 
          +if chemistry_plan else                                        
      145 +                       "O2-sensitive reaction"),              
      146 +        ))                                                    
      147 +        next_stream(prev_op, "deoxy_1")                       
      148 +        prev_op = "deoxy_1"                                   
      149 +                                                              
      150 +    # ── Photoreactor ────────────────────────────────────────
          +───────────────────                                           
      151 +    ops.append(UnitOperation(                                 
      152 +        op_id="reactor_1", op_type="coil_reactor",            
      153 +        label=f"{proposal.tubing_material} Photoreactor Coil",
      154 +        parameters={

      157 +            "volume_mL": proposal.reactor_volume_mL,

      159 +            "wavelength_nm": proposal.wavelength_nm,          
      160 +            "length_m": round(

      164 +        },                                                    
      165 +        required=True,                                        
      166 +        rationale="Photochemical flow reactor",               
      167 +    ))                                                        
      168 +    next_stream(prev_op, "reactor_1")                         
      169 +    prev_op = "reactor_1"                                     
      170 +                                                              
      171 +    # ── LED module (paired with reactor) ────────────────────
          +──────────────────                                            
      172 +    if proposal.wavelength_nm:                                
      173 +        ops.append(UnitOperation(                             
      174 +            op_id="led_1", op_type="led_module",              
      175 +            label=f"LED {proposal.wavelength_nm:.0f} nm",     
      176 +            parameters={                                      
      177 +                "wavelength_nm": proposal.wavelength_nm,      
      178 +                "setup": proposal.light_setup or "",          
      179 +            },                                                
      180 +            required=True,                                    
      181 +            rationale="Photoexcitation",                      
      182 +        ))                                                    
      183 +                                                              
      184 +    # ── BPR ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
          +──────────────────                                            
      185 +    if proposal.BPR_bar and proposal.BPR_bar > 0:             
      186 +        ops.append(UnitOperation(                             
      187 +            op_id="bpr_1", op_type="bpr",                     
      188 +            label="Back-Pressure Regulator",                  
      189 +            parameters={"pressure_bar": proposal.BPR_bar},    
      190 +            required=True,                                    
      191 +            rationale="Maintain pressurised liquid phase",    
      192 +        ))                                                    
      193 +        next_stream(prev_op, "bpr_1")                         
      194 +        prev_op = "bpr_1"                                     
      195 +                                                              
      196 +    # ── Post-reactor steps (quench etc.) ────────────────────
          +──────────────────                                            
      197 +    post_steps = proposal.post_reactor_steps or []            
      198 +    has_quench = any("quench" in s.lower() for s in post_steps
          +)                                                             
      199 +    if not has_quench and chemistry_plan and chemistry_plan.qu
          +ench_required:                                                
      200 +        post_steps = [f"Inline quench with {chemistry_plan.que
          +nch_reagent}"] + post_steps                                   
      201 +        has_quench = True                                     
      202 +                                                              
      203 +    if has_quench:                                            
      204 +        quench_label = next(                                  
      205 +            (s for s in post_steps if "quench" in s.lower()), 
      206 +            "Inline Quench"                                   
      207 +        )                                                     
      208 +        ops.append(UnitOperation(                             
      209 +            op_id="quench_1", op_type="quench_mixer",         
      210 +            label="Inline Quench",                            
      211 +            parameters={"reagent": quench_label},             
      212 +            required=True,                                    
      213 +            rationale=(chemistry_plan.quench_reasoning if chem
          +istry_plan else                                               
      214 +                       "Quench reactive intermediates"),      
      215 +        ))                                                    
      216 +        next_stream(prev_op, "quench_1")                      
      217 +        prev_op = "quench_1"                                  
      218 +                                                              
      219 +    # ── Collector ───────────────────────────────────────────
          +──────────────────                                            
      220 +    ops.append(UnitOperation(                                 
      221 +        op_id="collector_1", op_type="collector",             
      222 +        label="Product Collection",                           
      223 +        parameters={},                                        
      224 +        required=True,                                        
      225 +        rationale="Outlet",                                   
      226 +    ))                                                        
      227 +    next_stream(prev_op, "collector_1")                       
      228 +                                                              
      229 +    # ── PID description ─────────────────────────────────────
          +───────────────────                                           
      230 +    pid_parts = [op.label for op in ops if op.op_type != "led_
          +module"]                                                      
      231 +    pid = " → ".join(pid_parts)                               
      232 +                                                              
      233 +    return ProcessTopology(                                   
      234 +        topology_id="translate",                              
      235 +        unit_operations=ops,                                  
      236 +        streams=streams,

      240 +        pid_description=pid,                                  
      241 +        literature_support=[],                                
      242 +        topology_confidence=proposal.confidence,              
      243 +    )

❯ should we still keep the design module?                                       

● Yes, keep it — but they serve different purposes:

  FLORA-Translate — "I have a batch protocol, convert it to flow"
  - Input: existing batch conditions (temperature, time, catalyst, yield)
  - Output: flow equivalent of that specific protocol
  - Diagram: shows the actual chemicals from that batch reaction

  FLORA-Design — "I have a chemistry goal, design me a flow process from
  scratch"
  - Input: free-text goal ("design a flow process for Ru-photocatalyzed radical
  addition")
  - No batch protocol exists yet — you're starting from zero
  - Output: a full process design proposal from the literature corpus
  - Diagram: shows the suggested process with typical conditions for that
  reaction class
  - Also generates alternative topologies and yield vs residence time plots from
   corpus data

  The difference in practice:

  A researcher who already ran the reaction in batch uses Translate.

  A researcher planning a new flow campaign who hasn't done it in batch uses
  Design.

  They share the same ENGINE, ChromaDB corpus, and flowsheet builder — so
  there's no code duplication. The Design module adds the ChemistryClassifier +
  UnitOpSelector + TopologyAgent + ParameterAgent steps that Translate doesn't
  need (because Translate already has the conditions).

  Keep both. The overlap is in the underlying infrastructure, not the
  user-facing functionality.

❯ do you have any suggestion to make this agent better?                         

● Here are my suggestions organized by impact:

  ---
  Tier 1 — Highest impact (fix fundamental limitations)

  1. Feedback loop / correction memory
  Right now every query starts from zero. If a user corrects the agent
  ("actually the BPR should be 10 bar, not 5"), that correction disappears.
  Build a simple correction store — when users approve or reject proposals, save
   the feedback and weight it in future retrievals for similar reactions. A few
  hundred validated corrections would dramatically improve accuracy.

  2. Extraction quality audit
  Your entire RAG chain is only as good as the 140 extracted JSONs. Run a
  spot-check: take 10 papers, compare the extracted batch_baseline /
  flow_optimized against the actual paper, and measure how many fields are
  correctly extracted. If accuracy is below ~80%, the retrieval is retrieving
  noisy data. The extractor is the foundation — any garbage in it propagates
  through everything.

  3. Confidence-aware output
  Currently LOW confidence gives a warning but still returns a full proposal. It
   should instead return a "hypothesis mode" output that is visually distinct,
  explicitly says which fields have no literature support, and suggests what
  additional information the user should provide to get a better answer.

  ---
  Tier 2 — Architecture improvements

  4. Reaction-class-specific validators in ENGINE
  The current ChemistryValidator is general. For photoredox specifically, add:
  - Quantum yield check: if Φ is known and >0.5, flag that shorter residence
  times may be sufficient
  - Sensitizer check: if energy transfer photocatalysis, the triplet energy of
  sensitizer must exceed the substrate's triplet — this is checkable from the
  ChemistryPlan
  - Radical chain vs catalytic cycle distinction: chain reactions have different
   concentration requirements

  5. Multi-paper synthesis in Pass 5 of the extractor
  Right now each paper is extracted independently. But many papers report the
  same reaction with slightly different conditions. Build a
  deduplication/merging step that recognizes when two records describe the same
  chemistry and merges them into a higher-confidence composite record.

  6. Structured evaluation pipeline
  You need ground truth to know if the agent is improving or regressing. Build a
   small test set of 10-15 batch protocols where you know the correct flow
  translation (from published papers), and compute MAPE on the numerical fields.
   Run this every time you change the prompts. Without metrics, you're flying
  blind.

  ---
  Tier 3 — Feature additions

  7. Optimization space suggestion
  After translating batch → flow, add a step that suggests a Bayesian
  optimization space: "Based on literature, the key variables to screen are:
  residence time (5–20 min), temperature (25–60°C), photocatalyst loading (1–5
  mol%). Here is a suggested initial design of experiments." This directly
  connects to your stated goal of defining design spaces for BO.

  8. Scale-up reasoning
  Flow chemistry's main advantage is scalability. Add a scale_up field to the
  output: "To produce 10 g/day, you need Q = X mL/min for Y hours. With your
  current reactor (5 mL), that requires Z hours of continuous operation." This
  is simple arithmetic but extremely useful for planning.

  9. Interactive diagram editing
  The SVG diagram is static. Let users click on a node and edit a parameter
  (change BPR from 5 to 10 bar), then re-run the ENGINE validation without
  re-running the full LLM pipeline. This would make the tool much more useful
  for iterative design.

  10. Literature gap detector
  When confidence is LOW, instead of just saying "no analogies found", have the
  agent say specifically: "No flow chemistry papers found for [nitrene insertion
   + Ir photocatalysis]. The closest analogies are [X, Y] which differ in
  [mechanism/substrate class/solvent]. Here is what is uncertain and why." This
  is more actionable than a generic LOW confidence flag.

  ---
  Tier 4 — Long-term

  11. Connect to real-time literature
  Your corpus is 140 papers extracted once. Chemistry literature grows. Connect
  to Semantic Scholar or OpenAlex API to periodically fetch new papers matching
  your chemistry keywords, run them through the extractor, and add them to
  ChromaDB automatically. A growing corpus directly improves RAG quality over
  time.

  12. Experimental validation tracker
  Let users mark proposals as "tried in lab" and record actual vs predicted
  conditions. This creates a ground truth dataset that compounds over time.
  After 50 validated experiments, you can fine-tune the prompts or even
  fine-tune a small model on domain-specific batch→flow translations.

  ---
  My top 3 to implement next, in order:

  1. Evaluation pipeline — you need to know if the agent is working before
  adding features
  2. Feedback loop — captures user corrections, improves over time with zero
  extra effort
  3. BO design space suggestion — directly serves your stated research goal

SECTION 0 — OVERVIEW AND PHILOSOPHY                                             
FLORA (Flow Literature Oriented Retrieval Agent) is a web-based copilot for     
                                                                                
flow chemistry process design. The GUI is a Streamlit multipage application     
                                                                                
that exposes all user-facing modules in a clean, lab-tool aesthetic.            
Module map (what the GUI exposes):                                              
SECTION 1 — DESIGN                                                              
                                                                                
Batch-to-Flow     (FLORA-Translate)                                             
                                                                                
Process Design    (FLORA-Design)                                                
SECTION 2 — EVALUATE                                                            
                                                                                
Protocol Diagnostics  (ENGINE council, standalone)                              
                                                                                
Condition Optimization (Bayesian Optimization Helper)                           
SECTION 3 — KNOWLEDGE  [collapsible, admin-level]                               
                                                                                
Literature Mining     (SCOUT)                                                   
                                                                                
Knowledge Extraction  (PRISM)                                                   
                                                                                
Knowledge Base        (Corpus Browser)                                          
Backend modules (NOT shown in GUI, called silently):                            
                                                                                
engine/             — ENGINE council, used by Translate + Design + Diagnose     
                                                                                
data/chroma_db/     — ChromaDB vector store                                     
                                                                                
data/lab_inventory.json                                                         
Design principles:                                                              
·    Clean, minimal aesthetic — no gradients, no animations, no emoji overload  
·    Every output downloadable (PNG, JSON, CSV)                                 
·    Every design decision traceable to a literature source                     
·    Mobile-unfriendly is acceptable — this is a desktop lab tool               
·    Load time < 3s for all pages (heavy calls behind spinner)                  
·    Never show raw Python errors to the user — always catch and display        
                                                                                
a clean error card with a suggested fix

FLORA — Flow Literature Oriented Retrieval Agent                                
A web-based copilot for flow chemistry process design.                          
Modules                                                                         
Module    Purpose                                                               
FLORA-Translate    Convert a batch protocol to a flow process                   
FLORA-Design    Design a flow process from a chemistry goal

  1. Executive summary — what FLORA does in one paragraph with a concrete
  example

  rationale

  7. Data flow — how papers become queryable knowledge
  8. Dashboard — all 7 pages summarised
  9. Tech stack — clean table
  10. Limitations + roadmap — honest about what doesn't work yet
  11. How to run — 5 commands

  It's written for a technical audience (company leadership / collaborators) —
  conceptual focus, no code snippets, clear diagrams.
